2006 Dodge Magnum 3.5L V6 AWD. Car is in pretty good shape, lots of new parts from previous owner and myself trying to fix a stutter. This car runs and drives great when cold, but when at operating temp, develops a random hesitation/stutter seemingly only on acceleration. Still idles fine hot or cold. I'm just an amateur mechanic and I checked or replaced everything I know to check. This one has me stumped! It has to be something simple, but I just don't have the tools. A proper diagnostic scanner or reader would be a plus. Good solid car, and easy money if you can figure out the issue. I'm done with it. Asking 1500 no trades at this time.

Cam position sensor
